Action mapping used by the checker (for your reference):

- (OPENOBJECT ?r)           ->  open <r>
- (PICKUPOBJECT ?o ?r)      ->  take <o> from <r>
- (PUTOBJECT ?o ?r)         ->  move <o> to <r>
- (USEOBJECT ?o)            ->  use <o>
- (HEATOBJECT ?o ?mw)       ->  heat <o> with <mw>
- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>

Current DF (seed to minimally edit):
|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

|DF_END|

Action mapping used by the checker (for your reference):
- (GOTOLOCATION ?from ?to)  ->  go to <to>
- (OPENOBJECT ?r)           ->  open <r>
- (PICKUPOBJECT ?o ?r)      ->  take <o> from <r>
- (PUTOBJECT ?o ?r)         ->  move <o> to <r>
- (USEOBJECT ?o)            ->  use <o>
- (HEATOBJECT ?o ?mw)       ->  heat <o> with <mw>
- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>

Current DF (seed to minimally edit):
|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

Action mapping used by the checker (for your reference):

- (OPENOBJECT ?r)           ->  open <r>
- (PICKUPOBJECT ?o ?r)      ->  take <o> from <r>
- (PUTOBJECT ?o ?r)         ->  move <o> to <r>
- (USEOBJECT ?o)            ->  use <o>
- (HEATOBJECT ?o ?mw)       ->  heat <o> with <mw>
- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>

Current DF (seed to minimally edit):
|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

SUGGESTED_GOAL_LITERAL: (at countertop1)

Action mapping used by the checker (for your reference):
- (GOTOLOCATION ?from ?to)  ->  go to <to>
- (OPENOBJECT ?r)           ->  open <r>
- (PICKUPOBJECT ?o ?r)      ->  take <o> from <r>
- (PUTOBJECT ?o ?r)         ->  move <o> to <r>
- (USEOBJECT ?o)            ->  use <o>
- (HEATOBJECT ?o ?mw)       ->  heat <o> with <mw>
- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>

Current DF (seed to minimally edit):
|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing

    sharpObject - object
  )

    (at ?r - receptacle)

    (cleaned ?o - object)

    (sliced ?o - object)

  )

    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))

Note on naming:
- In DF/PF, object names should be lowercase with spaces removed (e.g., "armchair 1" -> armchair1).

Current DF (seed to minimally edit):
|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

Goal hint (you may use this exact goal literal):
SUGGESTED_GOAL_LITERAL: (holding pan1)

Action mapping used by the checker (for your reference):
- (GOTOLOCATION ?from ?to)  ->  go to <to>
- (OPENOBJECT ?r)           ->  open <r>
- (PICKUPOBJECT ?o ?r)      ->  take <o> from <r>
- (PUTOBJECT ?o ?r)         ->  move <o> to <r>
- (USEOBJECT ?o)            ->  use <o>
- (HEATOBJECT ?o ?mw)       ->  heat <o> with <mw>
- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>
- (COOLOBJECT ?o ?fridge)   ->  cool <o> with <fridge>

Current DF (seed to minimally edit):
|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

Goal hint (you may use this exact goal literal):
SUGGESTED_GOAL_LITERAL: (holding ladle1)

Action mapping used by the checker (for your reference):
- (GOTOLOCATION ?from ?to)  ->  go to <to>
- (OPENOBJECT ?r)           ->  open <r>
- (PICKUPOBJECT ?o ?r)      ->  take <o> from <r>
- (PUTOBJECT ?o ?r)         ->  move <o> to <r>
- (USEOBJECT ?o)            ->  use <o>
- (HEATOBJECT ?o ?mw)       ->  heat <o> with <mw>
- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>
- (COOLOBJECT ?o ?fridge)   ->  cool <o> with <fridge>

Current DF (seed to minimally edit):
|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  )
  (:action PutObject

  )

- (OPENOBJECT ?r)           ->  open <r>

- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

- (USEOBJECT ?o)            ->  use <o>
- (HEATOBJECT ?o ?mw)       ->  heat <o> with <mw>
- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>
- (COOLOBJECT ?o ?fridge)   ->  cool <o> with <fridge>
- (SLICEOBJECT ?r ?co ?k)   ->  slice <co> with <k>

- In DF/PF, object names should be lowercase with spaces removed (e.g., "armchair 1" -> armchair1).

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

- (HEATOBJECT ?o ?mw)       ->  heat <o> with <mw>
- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

- (USEOBJECT ?o)            ->  use <o>

- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

- (CLEANOBJECT ?o ?sink)    ->  clean <o> with <sink>
- (COOLOBJECT ?o ?fridge)   ->  cool <o> with <fridge>
- (SLICEOBJECT ?r ?co ?k)   ->  slice <co> with <k>

- In DF/PF, object names should be lowercase with spaces removed (e.g., "armchair 1" -> armchair1).

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

    :effect (on ?o)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )

  )

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)
|DF_END|

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

|DF_START|
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
